  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2addb0cf-4123-4197-94cc-c0e0fbe20963'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer10647005721316063359">Clarissa Moone’s a smart, quirky art history grad with an almost unhealthy obsession for vintage clothes.   <span id="freeText10647005721316063359" style="display:none">Clarissa Moone’s a smart, quirky art history grad with an almost unhealthy obsession for vintage clothes. When she lands a job working for the enigmatic Aidan Thornhill, she doesn’t quite know what to expect—but certainly not romance.<br /><br />Aidan is a self-made billionaire whose early life is shrouded in mystery. Fleeing a scandal, he joined the army and, years later, returned from Afghanistan with a head full of bad memories and a million dollars left to him by a dead friend. Now, he’s one of LA’s wealthiest bachelors—and he’s also smoking hot. <br /><br />But even this billionaire veteran didn’t count on the voluptuous Clarissa. With rumors already circulating, Aidan breaks his golden rule: one steamy night on his private yacht, he seduces Clarissa. When he discovers her lack of experience, instead of running, he takes control. Things are about to get filthier than Clarissa ever imagined.<br /><br />Aidan’s dark past is never far behind. Determined to stir trouble, three figures—an old army comrade, a spurned ex-con, and a spoiled old flame with sharp claws—emerge to reap revenge.<br /><br />Rising to defend his new lover, the former soldier charges headlong into battle, determined to have Clarissa even if it means losing everything, while she must choose whether to ignore the rumors and continue to bathe in Aidan’s charms… Or leave her dream job.</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2764754274?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lindsey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lindsey" href="/user/show/7139602-lindsey">Lindsey</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39306452-entrance">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2764754274" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8312415551244493683">I hated giving this series such a low rating but I had a very hard time getting past the general feel of the series. The characters were all great but I really felt that if the author would have placed this in England or somewhere like that, it would have been a much better book. The series is based in LA and all of the characters, including the quirky best friend to Clarissa, all speak so "properly". That's fine as I am sure that there are some that speak that way all of the world but it never </span>
  <span id="freeText8312415551244493683" style="display:none">I hated giving this series such a low rating but I had a very hard time getting past the general feel of the series. The characters were all great but I really felt that if the author would have placed this in England or somewhere like that, it would have been a much better book. The series is based in LA and all of the characters, including the quirky best friend to Clarissa, all speak so "properly". That's fine as I am sure that there are some that speak that way all of the world but it never fit for me. There were several times as I was reading each book in the series that I had to double check where they were living as it all just felt so off. I probably will not ready anything else from this author for that reason. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8312415551244493683" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8177104491387552440">Entrance<br/>By JJ Sorel <br/>Thornhill Trilogy Book 1<br/>Narrated by Mehgan Andrzejewski, Thomas Hart<br/><br/>What happens when your reputation precedes you? Aiden Thornhill's new assistant is beautiful and smart. She does not impress easily, but there is something about her new boss that catches her eye. Maybe it's the ease of conversation, or his incredible eyes. When the chance arises, the two become an item. But secrets are kept, and as we know, they always come to surface. As Clarissa thinks she is getting to kn</span>
  <span id="freeText8177104491387552440" style="display:none">Entrance<br />By JJ Sorel <br />Thornhill Trilogy Book 1<br />Narrated by Mehgan Andrzejewski, Thomas Hart<br /><br />What happens when your reputation precedes you? Aiden Thornhill's new assistant is beautiful and smart. She does not impress easily, but there is something about her new boss that catches her eye. Maybe it's the ease of conversation, or his incredible eyes. When the chance arises, the two become an item. But secrets are kept, and as we know, they always come to surface. As Clarissa thinks she is getting to know her new boyfriend, more information about his past keeps cropping up. Where will this relationship go? I am enjoying this story. A lot. Yes, it's got steamy scenes, but the complexity of the characters is what I truly enjoy. Clarissa is quirky, enjoys vintage clothing and music and is just a fascinating character. She's not rich in money, but she has a lot of ambition, love and patience. Aiden is extremely complex. He is hiding something and I want to know what it is! Bits and pieces are coming out, but I can't wait til it all comes out. It's a cliffhanger, so I need to get the next book queued up and ready to go.<br /><br />Mehgan Andrzejewski and Thomas Hart narrate this story, and they are cast perfectly. Meghan gives that quirkiness to Clarissa, adds some spunk and emotions, and even has us wanting to give her a good shake once in a while. She brings out all her eccentricities. Hart becomes Aiden, with his charismatic voice, sucking Clarissa in and understandably so.I enjoyed this combination of voices and look forward to book 2.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8177104491387552440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2236614250" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2236614250" />
    <a title="J.R. Tyger" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26288955-j-r-tyger"><img alt="J.R. Tyger" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442955036p2/26288955.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2236614250?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J.R. Tyger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J.R. Tyger" href="/user/show/26288955-j-r-tyger">J.R. Tyger</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2236614250" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9977383133788095088">Clarissa Moone - She majored in Art History in college. She spent time looking for a job, when her credit card is to the max, with a temp/job agency in LA, when they call her to attend an interview to be a personal assistant. They gave her the address in Malibu to a mansion that she fell in love with when she arrived as she did for the artwork when she got inside. Upon getting there, Greta Thornhill came out and told them, Clarissa and the other applicants, that they were to answer one question </span>
  <span id="freeText9977383133788095088" style="display:none">Clarissa Moone - She majored in Art History in college. She spent time looking for a job, when her credit card is to the max, with a temp/job agency in LA, when they call her to attend an interview to be a personal assistant. They gave her the address in Malibu to a mansion that she fell in love with when she arrived as she did for the artwork when she got inside. Upon getting there, Greta Thornhill came out and told them, Clarissa and the other applicants, that they were to answer one question for this interview and that they only had five minutes. When Greta collects her's she eyes her up and down. They are told that someone will be in touch soon. Not long after she returns home and questions thrown at her by her roommate, Tabitha, her best friend since kids, the agency calls and informs her that she has offered the position for Mr. Thornhill's PA. She readily accepts the position. It's when she arrives to sign paperwork and contracts to start working that she runs into her boss unbeknownst to her. She mistakes Aidan, as she never gets his name and she never sees his eyes behind the sunglasses and hat that he wears, for the gardener. She only meets him because his dog comes running up to her. She meets him again like that after she has started her job and is at the beach one afternoon. It wasn't until the gala she had been prepping for her first two weeks that she finally figures out that the guy she met with his dog was actually Aidan Thornhill, her boss. All that night she notices him staring at her everytime her eyes went in his direction. And that made her hot for him. But when he invited her onto his yacht a day or so later she was nervous to be seen with him. For it to be known that they might be seen together as she was told by another worker not to fall in love with him and that he was a lady's man.<br /><br />Aidan Thornhill - Billionaire extraordinaire caught sight of Clarissa during the interview where he was watching so no one could see him. Her answer her question was even better than expected. He was smitten. It didn't take him long to feel more for her but only when her phone died, when was to be in New York on business but flew back, he was out looking for her and found her out with her friend, her friend's newest boyfriend and his friend. He thinks he is wrong about how she felt and that she might be using him. Until she follows him out of the restaurant to talk to him. They spend the night together before he heads back to New York to finish business. When he gets back they spend a glorious weekend together before he jets off to Germany for two weeks for more business and she finishes getting the gala prepared. The gala is where Clarissa meets Aidan ex-fiancee. Jessica, the ex, tells her some things about Aidan he hadn't yet divulged in yet that has her running.<br /><br />I thoroughly enjoyed this book. I'm intrigued to find out what else happens in the second part when it's released. I can't wait. I love that Clarissa has a 1960's vintage taste in clothing, though I do not wear the style, I love the era.<br /><br />What I didn't like about the book was it being too formal in dialect. I have never heard anyone in LA or CA mind you, speak as if they grew up in a different time period and a different country. I believed one should use the dialect of the area in which they are writing and the area in which the character was raised. This is fiction after all and not one person I know speaks with perfect grammar 100% of the time.<br /><br />Other than that, I'm in love. To find someone who has a heart like Aidan is almost unheard of these days. Sorel, you are setting high standards for what a woman should look for in a man but that woman best appreciate having a man like Aidan if she gets herself a man like him. I can say that any guy that would read this should hold out for a soul like Clarissa's and he best appreciate her as well. By the way, can't wait for book two. I'm excited to know where the story will take me next.<br /><br />***Received an ARC for my honest review. Thank you***</span>
  <a data-text-id="9977383133788095088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2209505233" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2209505233" />
    <a title="Jewel Hart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart"><img alt="Jewel Hart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595707974p2/56470711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2209505233?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jewel Hart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jewel Hart" href="/user/show/56470711-jewel-hart">Jewel Hart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2209505233" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5094393427955258933">In this sizzling contemporary romance story, J.J. Sorel, brings readers an emotional, intriguing and unique love story. The story begins with, Clarissa Moone, sitting in an expensive fancy office amidst a handful of, model worthy, beautiful women. She is timidly awaiting for her name to be called for an interview for a new personal assistant job. Not knowing who her new boss is, she has no idea that she is about to embark on a life and love she never expected or could dream of.<br/><br/>The next day, she </span>
  <span id="freeText5094393427955258933" style="display:none">In this sizzling contemporary romance story, J.J. Sorel, brings readers an emotional, intriguing and unique love story. The story begins with, Clarissa Moone, sitting in an expensive fancy office amidst a handful of, model worthy, beautiful women. She is timidly awaiting for her name to be called for an interview for a new personal assistant job. Not knowing who her new boss is, she has no idea that she is about to embark on a life and love she never expected or could dream of.<br /><br />The next day, she lands the job. She goes from being penniless, to actually living at her new boss’s opulent multimillion dollar estate. She is now surrounded with beautiful things, exquisite art, and her extremely handsome new boss, Aiden. Being an art history major and art lover, she can’t believe her luck.<br /><br />Aiden, falls for smart, voluptuous and beautiful Clarissa at first sight. Although, Clarissa sees herself as an average normal girl, Aiden sees a classy, intelligent and desirable woman. For these reasons, Aiden falls hard for Clarissa. And for Clarissa, she feels the same about Aiden, and tingles when he glances at her. Aiden has a somewhat shady past, but Clarissa doesn’t seem to care, she is too taken by him.<br /><br />What ensues is an emotional, lustful love story between two people that must overcome the past and try to make it work.<br /><br />J.J. Sorel has done a magnificent job in her first book, Entrance, in the Thornhill Trilogy. The passionate love scenes are tastefully written and described. I was thrilled and excited while reading this delicious romance story. Sorel’s voice is clearly heard and quite unique. <br /><br />The descriptions of everything from Aiden’s estate, to the food and to the love scenes, took me on a delightful sensory ride. The dialog is written well, engaging the reader with every word. J.J. Sorel seizes the reader with a balmy story of love, lust and relationships. She is a skillful writer with a grand imagination that comes alive on paper. She has proven herself in this impressive novel. <br /><br />Entrance is so much more than a sexual love story.<br />Sorel shows how difficult relationships can be when the past, gossip, vengeance, love, desire and other people are involved. This story is intelligent, realistic and exciting. This is one of those books that I would read again. I highly recommend it to all those that love smart and simmering adult romance novels.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5094393427955258933" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3557155642?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39306452-entrance">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4169697-tinamarie?shelf=bdsm-erotica">bdsm-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4169697-tinamarie?shelf=not-my-cuppa">not-my-cuppa</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3557155642&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3557155642" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7367605296449705241">Listened to audio book narrated by Mehgan Andrzejewski and Thomas Hart. I enjoyed Hart's narration it came across very clean. I found myself wishing he had more narration time. I'm not sure if it's Andrzejewski's voice or the story but her narration for Clarissa come across as extremely young and naive at times and I wasn't a fan. There were several noticeable audio volume inconsistencies as well.<br/><br/>Aidan Thornhill is a self-made billionaire and a former Ranger with Special Forces in Afghanistan. H</span>
  <span id="freeText7367605296449705241" style="display:none">Listened to audio book narrated by Mehgan Andrzejewski and Thomas Hart. I enjoyed Hart's narration it came across very clean. I found myself wishing he had more narration time. I'm not sure if it's Andrzejewski's voice or the story but her narration for Clarissa come across as extremely young and naive at times and I wasn't a fan. There were several noticeable audio volume inconsistencies as well.<br /><br />Aidan Thornhill is a self-made billionaire and a former Ranger with Special Forces in Afghanistan. He's keeps to himself avoiding the limelight while trying to help worthwhile causes. He has a lot of secrets in his closet and his past threatens his future.<br /><br />Twenty-one year old virgin, Clarissa Moone has been hired to be Aidan's PA and is specifically told NOT to fall for Aidan. She's a brilliant art historian major with many talents. When she meets the sexy 'gardener' with the dog on the property her fantasies run wild and she's in deep when she realizes it's actually Aidan.<br /><br />This book is filled with hot steamy sex, and secrets. But everything felt very over the top. Aidan has so many issues it's a wonder he's even functional. Clarrissa and her friend's immaturity made me feel like I'm reading about high school teenagers, not an intelligent adult woman. Her friend's advice went from supportive one minute to sabotaging and catty the next, but Clarissa is oblivious. <br /><br />When settling in for an erotic falling for your billionaire boss read, it's hard to stay in the fantasy with the constant reminders about losing her job, it started to weird me out. While I appreciated that Aidan loved a natural woman, it felt like the author was taking digs at any woman that had any work done. The first time was okay, but the repeated digs started to feel mean.<br /><br />Their story isn't resolved at the end of this book and many things are left dangling for future books to resolve. I wanted to like this book but I just didn't.<br /><br /><br />I received this audiobook at no-cost from Audiobookworm Promotions. The gifting of this audiobook did not affect my opinion of it. If you like my reviews I hope you will follow my blog. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://wyldheartreads.wordpress.com/">https://wyldheartreads.wordpress.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_2227621765" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2227621765" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8757941-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1548808771p2/8757941.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2227621765?book_show_action=true">Dec 26, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/8757941-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8757941-jen?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8757941-jen?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2227621765" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16113193883809730758">I really enjoyed Entrance by J.J. Sorel. As the first book in a trilogy, I thought this book did a great job creating the world the rest of the books will take place in, and the reader meets so many interesting characters; I could definitely see this becoming much more than just a trilogy given all the couples/potential couples introduced in just this novel.<br/><br/>Clarissa meets billionaire Aidan after taking a job as his charity-event-planning PA. Neither knew that their love for art would catapult th</span>
  <span id="freeText16113193883809730758" style="display:none">I really enjoyed Entrance by J.J. Sorel. As the first book in a trilogy, I thought this book did a great job creating the world the rest of the books will take place in, and the reader meets so many interesting characters; I could definitely see this becoming much more than just a trilogy given all the couples/potential couples introduced in just this novel.<br /><br />Clarissa meets billionaire Aidan after taking a job as his charity-event-planning PA. Neither knew that their love for art would catapult them both into a steamy romance that neither ever expected to experience. Of course, both have less-than-perfect pasts: Aidan threw himself first into a sex addiction and then into the Army Special Forces when his mother chose drugs over him; Clarissa's mom died when she was young, and she's found herself very sheltered - until Aidan, that is. Now, with Clarissa by his side, Aidan can finally put the past behind him and find a new sense of peace and wholeness.<br /><br />The writing overall was good; there were a few romantic scenes I had to slow down for in order to properly follow what was going on, but other than that, the writing was spot on, detailed, and told the story well. Characters were developed, no matter how much page time they received. Both Aidan's and Clarissa's backstories were detailed, were more than just a mere mention, and contributed to the present and future of both main characters. I thought the story worked well, and I really appreciated the fact that this book contained a full story instead of leaving the reader with a cliffhanger leading into book 2 of the trilogy. Overall, this is a great read for anyone wanting a sweet yet steamy romance featuring an innocent woman and a former-military billionaire who wants to give his woman the world.<br /><br />I received an ARC of this book in exchange for an honest review.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2813272576" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2813272576" />
    <a title="Wendy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8109701-wendy"><img alt="Wendy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421030322p2/8109701.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2813272576?book_show_action=true">May 08, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy" href="/user/show/8109701-wendy">Wendy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/39306452-entrance">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2813272576" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11900867914478908210">This book is like an X rated Disney movie. Everyone is so perfect and speak only in proper, well groomed English. Almost everything in this book is a cliché. My main issues that ruined this book for me are these:<br/><br/>1) I hate it when the hero is so inhumanly beautiful and hot that, at first glance, ever human female on earth will melt and fall completely in love with him. Really? Give me a brake! That’s the case here. He can’t even talk to a woman without her swooning and lusting over him. Poor guy.</span>
  <span id="freeText11900867914478908210" style="display:none">This book is like an X rated Disney movie. Everyone is so perfect and speak only in proper, well groomed English. Almost everything in this book is a cliché. My main issues that ruined this book for me are these:<br /><br />1) I hate it when the hero is so inhumanly beautiful and hot that, at first glance, ever human female on earth will melt and fall completely in love with him. Really? Give me a brake! That’s the case here. He can’t even talk to a woman without her swooning and lusting over him. Poor guy. Most of his past PAs, who he rarely sees, are fired or quit because they fall in love and try to jump him. Not only is he uber handsome, he’s also uber wealthy, uber nice, and uber uber generous. AKA Prince Charming. Even his “issues” seemed staged.<br /><br />2) I hate a heroin who is a virgin in her 20’s because she’s never felt attracted to a man enough to want to have sex with him, then suddenly, is drowning in intense lust at first sight of the unearthly beautiful hero. And of course, she is exquisite beautiful. She’s every man’s fantasy and they all in love with her and her big D cups, which are mentioned on every page.<br /><br />3) I hate coincidences that feel completely fake and unreal. Although this is a small thing it still bugs me. Here, the heroine like to dress in a 1960’s retro style. Fine. But guess what, so does her boss. Not only that, the heroines father and boss are also immediately hot for each other. And then there’s the dog.<br /><br />4) The writing. What to say. The author was obviously British since there were many common British words and phrases used that we don’t say here. I also hated the expression “boy”, and the talk about tummies. At one point, prince charming actually said his tummy hurt. Really? And why is the word “sensitive” used a thousand times? And then there were the sex scenes. They were just as bad.<br /><br />Overall, this book was a flop!</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13868426833050377742">A hot contemporary romance, J.J. Sorel introduces her audience to Clarissa Moone and her new hot hot hot boss Aidan.  Aidan has a murky past but Clarissa doesn’t really care, her skin sizzles when he’s nearby and her breath is taken when he touches her.  <br/><br/>Aidan, quiet and conservative finds himself falling for Clarissa at first sight!  Aidan is treading where he has never been before – a beautiful, quiet woman with a smile that removes all darkness.  Her virginal body and engaging intelligence se</span>
  <span id="freeText13868426833050377742" style="display:none">A hot contemporary romance, J.J. Sorel introduces her audience to Clarissa Moone and her new hot hot hot boss Aidan.  Aidan has a murky past but Clarissa doesn’t really care, her skin sizzles when he’s nearby and her breath is taken when he touches her.  <br /><br />Aidan, quiet and conservative finds himself falling for Clarissa at first sight!  Aidan is treading where he has never been before – a beautiful, quiet woman with a smile that removes all darkness.  Her virginal body and engaging intelligence send him into a lustful desire and passion.<br /><br />Together they must explore their relationship amidst gossip, lust, revenge and more.  This is a story where love and passion must win but will the past allow them to do so? <br /><br />J.J. Sorel’s Entrance is an engaging read for anyone who enjoys contemporary romance.  Well written, Sorel details the story in an engaging manner and vividly describes the characters and their actions to perfection.  The romance scenes are not overdone, rather they are written in a tasteful and realistic style.  It is emotional and satisfying, yet describes accurately the doubts and struggles couples have in their relationships at times.<br /><br />I enjoyed how each chapter identified who the voice was so the viewpoints were clear.  It also allowed her audience a clearer view of each person. Sorel knows how to captivate her audience and provide an absorbing tale of love, sex, and relationships.  Masterful storyteller, Sorel gives her audience what they want in a bewitching style. </span>
  <a data-text-id="13868426833050377742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

While Aiden means well, he has never felt the way he feels about Clary so he is trying to figure things out as he goes. <span id="freeTextContainer18053426893570738577">A beautiful Billionaire love story. Aidan Thornhill is a billionaire who likes his privacy, shares his wealth with those who need it most, and is very down to earth. He is in search of a PA to help plan and run the gala's that he has to raise money for the various charities that he runs to help the needy.   <span id="freeText18053426893570738577" style="display:none">A beautiful Billionaire love story. Aidan Thornhill is a billionaire who likes his privacy, shares his wealth with those who need it most, and is very down to earth. He is in search of a PA to help plan and run the gala's that he has to raise money for the various charities that he runs to help the needy. His Aunt is his closest confidant and works with him in running his charities. <br /><br />Clarissa Moone has been contacted by an employment agency to go to an interview for the position. She was just an after thought by the company, but she was very hopeful that she would get the job. Clarissa is an eccentric 21 year old, she has a degree in Art History, and is a caring thoughtful person. She is not a woman to watch the media, or gossip rags about celebrities. So when she goes to the interview, she is not aware of who the man is that she will be working for, until she gets home and talks with her roommate and best friend since childhood, Tabitha, who knows about everyone.<br /><br />I loved this story and the characters really drew me in. I love Aidan and Clarissa, but Greta and Julian add so much to this story as well. They are the people who help to make Aidan and Clarissa who they are as adults. They care for them and they are very much a part of their lives. <br /><br />I look forward to reading more of the Thornhill Trilogy in the coming year. JJ Sorel is a new to me author and I look forward to reading more of her stories. </span>

  <span id="freeText15801615881009346204" style="display:none">This book reads like a teenager wrote it. The main character gets a job throwing fancy parties and is just handed wealth because she's so nice. Seriously. She got a job cause she was nice and every other woman that applied was just looking for a rich husband or sex with a billionaire (but wait...). It's alarming how much derision and judgment comes out towards all women not the main character. Clarissa is clearly "not like other girls" because ALL other girls, including her bestie, are shitty for various reasons-mostly slut-shaming. To to it off, the obsession with being vintage is exhaustingly boring. <br /><br />It's clear the writer has some real disgusting views of women but she also let loose some about men with the absurd idea that a man who trained really hard for the Army would have leftover muscles... Because going to the gym is clearly a character flaw. <br /><br />I couldn't finish the book. It was too absurd to be enjoyable. It took so long for nothing to happen and I didn't even get to a single bit of conflict after over 1/3 of the book.</span>

The story between Clarissa and Aiden flowed perfectly with lots of intrigue, the plot was intriguing and you definitely wanted to know all the way through what was going to happen next.   <span id="freeText9467518492554783381" style="display:none">Life is the Ultimate Gift. This superb book kept me riveted from start to finish. I have never read a JJ Sorel book before but hey she is one heck of a good writer. The story between Clarissa and Aiden flowed perfectly with lots of intrigue, the plot was intriguing and you definitely wanted to know all the way through what was going to happen next. The story was erotic, romantic, and of course you have to have quite a few baddies in the story who are trying to blackmail the dark character of Aiden as well as the naive Clarissa. This book was beautifully written and I highly recommend this as a must read. It’s part one of a series and I hope I can read the next upcoming book. I could go on about this book but hate to give spoilers away to other readers. What really intrigued me most of all was what this author doesn’t know about fine arts is not worth knowing. Fantastic job JJ and hope I can do more reviews for this really good writer. This is my honest review of an ARC I received.</span>

  <span id="freeText8309628746889455434" style="display:none">I received an arc of this book from the publishers via NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. <br /><br />Clarissa is an art graduate but unable to find a job she is working temp jobs when she is sent to interview for a personal assistant position. Aidan Thornhill made his millions after military service which left deep scars in his mind. He is unable to resist the draw of his new personal assistant even though he has enough to concern himself with. <br /><br />This book started out with a lot of promise but I found it a little too slow and the plot line too predictable. The author is clearly a fan of fifty shades of grey, while not bdsm there are definite similarities in the plot. As several other reviewers have pointed Regency era speak is the dialogue format which is not fitting with a modern era setting. For fans of fifty shades of grey, I would definitely recommend this book. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16556271540113120520">Clarissa lands a job as the PA for a billionaire, and it all gets complicated. Aidan has LOTS of baggage in his past, and he seems to think the peel like an onion approach is best. While great for plotting, Aidan keeps letting other people tell Clarissa his secrets. If she wasn't so nauseatingly smitten, she would have smacked him upside the head and demanded the rest of his secrets by now. But other than Aidan's lack of upfront communication, the only real issue I have with this book is that th</span>
  <span id="freeText16556271540113120520" style="display:none">Clarissa lands a job as the PA for a billionaire, and it all gets complicated. Aidan has LOTS of baggage in his past, and he seems to think the peel like an onion approach is best. While great for plotting, Aidan keeps letting other people tell Clarissa his secrets. If she wasn't so nauseatingly smitten, she would have smacked him upside the head and demanded the rest of his secrets by now. But other than Aidan's lack of upfront communication, the only real issue I have with this book is that they keep saying that everyone is sensitive. First of all, if you are going to have sensitive characters running around your book, show don't tell...every other chapter. Second, being sensitive is not a blanket excuse for every decision you make. <br /><br />But I still enjoyed the plot, the cast of characters is interesting, and I can't wait for book 2! </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('AFHkIPjkZilZnHZJ+bCXjKoJ2Y6K8qk/622gIpWGis20l9Otk8G8tRK3v9il2zFQSRU1kJnbz6mZ6HarUfJxeg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FU8VHGmnVbsvc5cmUbrPsDIwh0AvYxQc0ZFpDJvnV7uhiSKRAoKPJ2RYXrcN0Wls0SxrXjxKcoqjFL+FX5OsDA==')})
  }

His account of his rise from a self-described below-average student, to becoming a poster boy for the ambitious, successful young entrepreneur, to nearly destroying himself in the process is the subject of A Practical Way to Get Rich . . . and Die Trying. Roa\'s twenty-year-long journey from being dead-broke to wealth he never imagined is an absurd and often comical story of talent, luck, risk, rapidly changing technology, larger-than-life personalities, sex, gambling, and excessive alcohol and drug consumption. Roa\'s intention for his memoir is not to present a glamorous rags-to-riches saga, but, instead, to serve as a cautionary tale of the toll that entrepreneurship can take on ambitious young people unprepared for the physical and mental costs that &quot;making it&quot; can take. Those pitfalls eventually took their toll on Roa, who, in the face of round-the-clock pressure and risk taking, ultimately suffered a psychotic breakdown from which he almost didn\'t walk away. As he healed in the aftermath, he began to question the ethos that had brought him to that dark place, and he learned from other entrepreneurs that they, too, had experienced similar debilitating issues that they felt unable to admit, let alone discuss.\n\nA Practical Way to Get Rich . . . and Die Trying is a compelling memoir and the foundation for a campaign of honesty and vulnerability in an industry that currently allows neither. Roa aims to be the bridge to helping young leaders confront the mental health issues and abuse that too often accompany the tech startup that so many have embraced as their salvation for their <span id="freeTextContainer5140197346020025630">J. J. Sorel whiles away her day writing Steamy Romance novels. She loves conjuring up slightly damaged, seductive men who fall madly in love with smart quirky women. Before becoming a writer ten years ago, she danced and choreographed for her supper. J. J. Sorel has written fourteen books, three of which never quite made it out alive from the dusty confines of her hard drive. Pretty soon she plans</span>
  <span id="freeText5140197346020025630" style="display:none">J. J. Sorel whiles away her day writing Steamy Romance novels. She loves conjuring up slightly damaged, seductive men who fall madly in love with smart quirky women. Before becoming a writer ten years ago, she danced and choreographed for her supper. J. J. Sorel has written fourteen books, three of which never quite made it out alive from the dusty confines of her hard drive. Pretty soon she plans to give birth to “A Taste of Peace.” A twisted love story about surfer by day, drummer by night, and billionaire by birth, Lachlan Peace, and his new admin assistant, Miranda Flowers. She only expected to get a job, not her slightly eccentric but very sexy boss, who also happens to live next door to the Thornhills. jjsorel.com<br /><br /></span>
